> **摘要**: 最近的进展证明了仅解码器大语言模型 (LLM) 在自动语音识别 (ASR) 方面的潜力。然而，在这个框架内实现流识别仍然是一个挑战。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种新颖的流式 ASR 方法，该方法将读/写策略网络与单调分块注意力 (MoChA) 相集成，以动态分段语音嵌入。这些片段在训练期间与标签序列交错，从而实现与法学硕士的无缝集成。在推理过程中，音频流会被缓冲，直到 MoChA 模块触发读取信号，此时缓冲的片段与前一个令牌一起被馈送到 LLM 中以进行下一个令牌预测。我们还引入了最小延迟训练目标，以引导策略网络实现准确的分割边界。此外，我们采用联合训练策略，其中非流式 LLM-ASR 模型和我们的流式模型共享参数。 AISHELL-1 和 AISHELL-2 普通话基准测试表明，我们的方法始终优于最近的流式 ASR 基准，分别实现了 5.1% 和 5.5% 的字符错误率。延迟优化使平均令牌生成延迟减少了 62.5%，对识别准确性的影响可以忽略不计
> **Abstract**: Recent advances have demonstrated the potential of decoderonly large language models (LLMs) for automatic speech recognition (ASR). However, enabling streaming recognition within this framework remains a challenge. In this work, we propose a novel streaming ASR approach that integrates a read/write policy network with monotonic chunkwise attention (MoChA) to dynamically segment speech embeddings. These segments are interleaved with label sequences during training, enabling seamless integration with the LLM. During inference, the audio stream is buffered until the MoChA module triggers a read signal, at which point the buffered segment together with the previous token is fed into the LLM for the next token prediction. We also introduce a minimal-latency training objective to guide the policy network toward accurate segmentation boundaries. Furthermore, we adopt a joint training strategy in which a non-streaming LLM-ASR model and our streaming model share parameters. Experiments on the AISHELL-1 and AISHELL-2 Mandarin benchmarks demonstrate that our method consistently outperforms recent streaming ASR baselines, achieving character error rates of 5.1% and 5.5%, respectively. The latency optimization results in a 62.5% reduction in average token generation delay with negligible impact on recognition accuracy

【4】Sylber 2.0: A Universal Syllable Embedding
- **标题**: Sylber 2.0：通用音节嵌入
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22306
> **作者**: Cheol Jun Cho,Nicholas Lee,Alan W Black,Gopala K. Anumanchipalli
> **摘要**: 扩展口语模型需要高效且通用的语音标记。最近的工作提出将音节作为低时间分辨率下有前途的语音标记，但现有模型仅限于英语并且无法捕获足够的声学细节。为了解决这一差距，我们提出了 Sylber 2.0，这是一种用于在音节级别对语音进行编码的自监督框架，可实现高效的时间压缩和高保真度重建。 Sylber 2.0 实现了 5 Hz 左右的极低标记频率，同时保留了多种语言和表达风格的语言和声学细节。实验表明，它的性能与之前在高频基线上运行的模型相当。此外，Sylber 2.0 支持高效的 TTS 建模，仅使用 72M 参数即可通过 SOTA 模型生成具有竞争力的清晰度和质量的语音。此外，Sylber 2.0 的通用性为低资源 ASR 提供​​了比以前的语音编码框架更有效的功能。总之，我们为一般口语建立了有效的音节级抽象。
> **Abstract**: Scaling spoken language modeling requires speech tokens that are both efficient and universal. Recent work has proposed syllables as promising speech tokens at low temporal resolution, but existing models are constrained to English and fail to capture sufficient acoustic detail. To address this gap, we present Sylber 2.0, a self-supervised framework for coding speech at the syllable level that enables efficient temporal compression and high-fidelity reconstruction. Sylber 2.0 achieves a very low token frequency around 5 Hz, while retaining both linguistic and acoustic detail across multiple languages and expressive styles. Experiments show that it performs on par with previous models operating on high-frequency baselines. Furthermore, Sylber 2.0 enables efficient TTS modeling which can generate speech with competitive intelligibility and quality with SOTA models using only 72M parameters. Moreover, the universality of Sylber 2.0 provides more effective features for low resource ASR than previous speech coding frameworks. In sum, we establish an effective syllable-level abstraction for general spoken language.

## 图像和视频处理(eess.IV:Image and Video Processing)

【1】Scale Equivariance Regularization and Feature Lifting in High Dynamic Range Modulo Imaging
- **标题**: 高动态范围模成像中的尺度等方差正则化和特征提升
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.23037
> **作者**: Brayan Monroy,Jorge Bacca
> **摘要**: 模成像通过循环包裹饱和强度来实现高动态范围 (HDR) 采集，但由于自然图像边缘和人工包裹不连续性之间的模糊性，准确重建仍然具有挑战性。这项工作提出了一种基于学习的 HDR 恢复框架，该框架包含两个关键策略：（i）在曝光变化下强制执行一致性的尺度等变正则化，以及（ii）结合原始模图像、包裹有限差分和闭合形式初始化的特征提升输入设计。这些组件共同增强了网络区分真实结构和包装伪影的能力，从而在感知和线性 HDR 质量指标上产生最先进的性能。
> **Abstract**: Modulo imaging enables high dynamic range (HDR) acquisition by cyclically wrapping saturated intensities, but accurate reconstruction remains challenging due to ambiguities between natural image edges and artificial wrap discontinuities. This work proposes a learning-based HDR restoration framework that incorporates two key strategies: (i) a scale-equivariant regularization that enforces consistency under exposure variations, and (ii) a feature lifting input design combining the raw modulo image, wrapped finite differences, and a closed-form initialization. Together, these components enhance the network's ability to distinguish true structure from wrapping artifacts, yielding state-of-the-art performance across perceptual and linear HDR quality metrics.

【2】Development of Domain-Invariant Visual Enhancement and Restoration (DIVER) Approach for Underwater Images
- **标题**: 水下图像领域不变视觉增强和恢复（DIVER）方法的开发
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22878
> **作者**: Rajini Makam,Sharanya Patil,Dhatri Shankari T M,Suresh Sundaram,Narasimhan Sundararajan
> **摘要**: 由于波长相关的衰减、散射和照明不均匀性（随水类型和深度的不同而变化），水下图像会遭受严重的退化。我们提出了一种无监督的域不变视觉增强和恢复（DIVER）框架，该框架将经验校正与物理引导建模相结合，以实现鲁棒的水下图像增强。 DIVER 首先应用 IlluminateNet 进行自适应亮度增强，或应用光谱均衡滤波器进行光谱归一化。然后，自适应光学校正模块使用通道自适应滤波来细化色调和对比度，而 Hydro-OpticNet 采用物理约束学习来补偿反向散射和波长相关的衰减。 IlluminateNet 和 Hydro-OpticNet 的参数通过使用复合损失函数的无监督学习进行优化。使用参考和非参考指标，在八个不同的数据集上对 DIVER 进行评估，这些数据集涵盖浅层、深层和高度浑浊的环境，包括自然低光和人工照明的场景。虽然 WaterNet、UDNet 和 Phaseformer 等最先进的方法在浅水中表现良好，但在深水中、光照不均匀或人工照明条件下，它们的性能会下降。相比之下，DIVER 在所有数据集上始终实现最佳或接近最佳的性能，展示了强大的域不变能力。 DIVER 比 UCIQE 中的 SOTA 方法至少提高了 9%。在低光 SeaThru 数据集上，调色板参考可以直接评估颜色恢复，与现有方法相比，DIVER 的 GPMAE 至少降低了 4.9%。除了视觉质量之外，DIVER 还通过增强基于 ORB 的关键点可重复性和匹配性能来提高机器人感知，确认其在不同水下环境中的稳健性。
> **Abstract**: Underwater images suffer severe degradation due to wavelength-dependent attenuation, scattering, and illumination non-uniformity that vary across water types and depths. We propose an unsupervised Domain-Invariant Visual Enhancement and Restoration (DIVER) framework that integrates empirical correction with physics-guided modeling for robust underwater image enhancement. DIVER first applies either IlluminateNet for adaptive luminance enhancement or a Spectral Equalization Filter for spectral normalization. An Adaptive Optical Correction Module then refines hue and contrast using channel-adaptive filtering, while Hydro-OpticNet employs physics-constrained learning to compensate for backscatter and wavelength-dependent attenuation. The parameters of IlluminateNet and Hydro-OpticNet are optimized via unsupervised learning using a composite loss function. DIVER is evaluated on eight diverse datasets covering shallow, deep, and highly turbid environments, including both naturally low-light and artificially illuminated scenes, using reference and non-reference metrics. While state-of-the-art methods such as WaterNet, UDNet, and Phaseformer perform reasonably in shallow water, their performance degrades in deep, unevenly illuminated, or artificially lit conditions. In contrast, DIVER consistently achieves best or near-best performance across all datasets, demonstrating strong domain-invariant capability. DIVER yields at least a 9% improvement over SOTA methods in UCIQE. On the low-light SeaThru dataset, where color-palette references enable direct evaluation of color restoration, DIVER achieves at least a 4.9% reduction in GPMAE compared to existing methods. Beyond visual quality, DIVER also improves robotic perception by enhancing ORB-based keypoint repeatability and matching performance, confirming its robustness across diverse underwater environments.

【3】Synthetic Abundance Maps for Unsupervised Super-Resolution of Hyperspectral Remote Sensing Images
- **标题**: 高光谱遥感图像无监督超分辨率合成丰度图
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22755
> **作者**: Xinxin Xu,Yann Gousseau,Christophe Kervazo,Saïd Ladjal
> **摘要**: 高光谱单图像超分辨率（HS-SISR）旨在增强高光谱图像的空间分辨率，以充分利用其光谱信息。虽然这一领域已经取得了相当大的进展，但大多数现有方法都是受到监督的，并且需要用于训练数据的地面实况数据，而这在实践中通常是无法获得的。为了克服这一限制，我们提出了一种基于合成丰度数据的新型 HS-SISR 无监督训练框架。该方法首先将高光谱图像分解为端元和丰度。然后训练神经网络仅使用合成丰度执行丰度超分辨率。这些合成丰度图是从死叶模型生成的，其特征继承自要超分辨率的低分辨率图像。随后使用经过训练的网络来增强原始图像丰度的空间分辨率，并通过将它们与端元组合来重建最终的超分辨率高光谱图像。实验结果证明了合成数据的训练价值和所提出方法的有效性。
> **Abstract**: Hyperspectral single image super-resolution (HS-SISR) aims to enhance the spatial resolution of hyperspectral images to fully exploit their spectral information. While considerable progress has been made in this field, most existing methods are supervised and require ground truth data for training-data that is often unavailable in practice. To overcome this limitation, we propose a novel unsupervised training framework for HS-SISR, based on synthetic abundance data. The approach begins by unmixing the hyperspectral image into endmembers and abundances. A neural network is then trained to perform abundance super-resolution using synthetic abundances only. These synthetic abundance maps are generated from a dead leaves model whose characteristics are inherited from the low-resolution image to be super-resolved. This trained network is subsequently used to enhance the spatial resolution of the original image's abundances, and the final super-resolution hyperspectral image is reconstructed by combining them with the endmembers. Experimental results demonstrate both the training value of the synthetic data and the effectiveness of the proposed method.

【4】Active Learning-Driven Lightweight YOLOv9: Enhancing Efficiency in Smart Agriculture
- **标题**: 主动学习驱动的轻量级YOLOv9：提升智慧农业效率
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22732
> **作者**: Hung-Chih Tu,Bo-Syun Chen,Yun-Chien Cheng
> **摘要**: 这项研究解决了温室环境中部署在边缘设备上的农业机器人实时检测西红柿和西红柿花的需求。在实际成像条件下，目标检测系统经常面临诸如摄像机距离变化引起的大规模变化、植物结构的严重遮挡以及高度不平衡的类别分布等挑战。这些因素使得依赖完全注释数据集的传统目标检测方法难以同时实现高检测精度和部署效率。为了克服这些限制，本研究提出了一种主动学习驱动的轻量级目标检测框架，集成了数据分析、模型设计和训练策略。首先，分析原始农业图像中物体的尺寸分布，重新定义操作目标范围，从而提高现实条件下的学习稳定性。其次，采用高效的特征提取模块来降低计算成本，同时引入轻量级注意力机制来增强多尺度和遮挡场景下的特征表示。最后，采用主动学习策略，在有限的标注预算下迭代选择高信息样本进行标注和训练，有效提高了少数和小目标类别的识别性能。实验结果表明，该方法在保持适合边缘设备部署的低参数数和推理成本的同时，有效提高了原始图像中西红柿和西红柿花的检测性能。在有限的注释条件下，该框架的整体检测精度达到了67.8% mAP，验证了其在智能农业应用中的实用性和可行性。
> **Abstract**: This study addresses the demand for real-time detection of tomatoes and tomato flowers by agricultural robots deployed on edge devices in greenhouse environments. Under practical imaging conditions, object detection systems often face challenges such as large scale variations caused by varying camera distances, severe occlusion from plant structures, and highly imbalanced class distributions. These factors make conventional object detection approaches that rely on fully annotated datasets difficult to simultaneously achieve high detection accuracy and deployment efficiency. To overcome these limitations, this research proposes an active learning driven lightweight object detection framework, integrating data analysis, model design, and training strategy. First, the size distribution of objects in raw agricultural images is analyzed to redefine an operational target range, thereby improving learning stability under real-world conditions. Second, an efficient feature extraction module is incorporated to reduce computational cost, while a lightweight attention mechanism is introduced to enhance feature representation under multi-scale and occluded scenarios. Finally, an active learning strategy is employed to iteratively select high-information samples for annotation and training under a limited labeling budget, effectively improving the recognition performance of minority and small-object categories. Experimental results demonstrate that, while maintaining a low parameter count and inference cost suitable for edge-device deployment, the proposed method effectively improves the detection performance of tomatoes and tomato flowers in raw images. Under limited annotation conditions, the framework achieves an overall detection accuracy of 67.8% mAP, validating its practicality and feasibility for intelligent agricultural applications.

【5】Training Beyond Convergence: Grokking nnU-Net for Glioma Segmentation in Sub-Saharan MRI
- **标题**: 超越收敛的训练：Grokking nnU-Net 在撒哈拉以南 MRI 中的神经胶质瘤分割
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22637
> **作者**: Mohtady Barakat,Omar Salah,Ahmed Yasser,Mostafa Ahmed,Zahirul Arief,Waleed Khan,Dong Zhang,Aondona Iorumbur,Confidence Raymond,Mohannad Barakat,Noha Magdy
> **摘要**: 神经胶质瘤给撒哈拉以南非洲地区（SSA）带来了越来越大的临床负担。在该地区，患者的中位生存期仍低于两年，并且获得诊断成像的机会极其有限。这些限制凸显了对自动化工具的迫切需求，这些工具可以从每次可用的扫描中提取尽可能多的信息，这些工具是针对本地数据进行专门训练的，而不是根据条件截然不同的高收入环境进行改编。我们利用脑肿瘤分割 (BraTS) Africa 2025 Challenge 数据集，这是一个专家注释的神经胶质瘤 MRI 集合。我们的目标是：(i) 在此数据集上使用 nnUNet 建立强大的基线，以及 (ii) 探索著名的“grokking”现象（从记忆到高级泛化的突然、后期训练跳跃）是否可以被触发，从而在没有额外标签的情况下提高性能。我们评估两种培训制度。第一种是快速、注重预算的方法，将优化限制在几个时期，这反映了非洲机构通常可用的 GPU 资源有限。尽管存在这一限制，nnUNet 仍取得了很高的 Dice 分数：整个肿瘤 (WH) 为 92.3%，肿瘤核心 (TC) 为 86.6%，增强肿瘤 (ET) 为 86.3%。第二种方案将训练延伸到远远超出收敛点的范围，旨在引发由神韵驱动的性能飞跃。通过这种方法，我们能够实现 grokking 并将我们的结果提高到更高的 Dice 分数：整个肿瘤 (WH) 为 92.2%，肿瘤核心 (TC) 为 90.1%，增强肿瘤 (ET) 为 90.2%。
> **Abstract**: Gliomas are placing an increasingly clinical burden on Sub-Saharan Africa (SSA). In the region, the median survival for patients remains under two years, and access to diagnostic imaging is extremely limited. These constraints highlight an urgent need for automated tools that can extract the maximum possible information from each available scan, tools that are specifically trained on local data, rather than adapted from high-income settings where conditions are vastly different. We utilize the Brain Tumor Segmentation (BraTS) Africa 2025 Challenge dataset, an expert annotated collection of glioma MRIs. Our objectives are: (i) establish a strong baseline with nnUNet on this dataset, and (ii) explore whether the celebrated "grokking" phenomenon an abrupt, late training jump from memorization to superior generalization can be triggered to push performance without extra labels. We evaluate two training regimes. The first is a fast, budget-conscious approach that limits optimization to just a few epochs, reflecting the constrained GPU resources typically available in African institutions. Despite this limitation, nnUNet achieves strong Dice scores: 92.3% for whole tumor (WH), 86.6% for tumor core (TC), and 86.3% for enhancing tumor (ET). The second regime extends training well beyond the point of convergence, aiming to trigger a grokking-driven performance leap. With this approach, we were able to achieve grokking and enhanced our results to higher Dice scores: 92.2% for whole tumor (WH), 90.1% for tumor core (TC), and 90.2% for enhancing tumor (ET).

【6】Bonnet: Ultra-fast whole-body bone segmentation from CT scans
- **标题**: Bonnet：通过 CT 扫描进行超快速全身骨骼分割
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22576
> **作者**: Hanjiang Zhu,Pedro Martelleto Rezende,Zhang Yang,Tong Ye,Bruce Z. Gao,Feng Luo,Siyu Huang,Jiancheng Yang
> **摘要**: 这项工作提出了 Bonnet，一种超快速稀疏体积管道，用于从 CT 扫描中进行全身骨骼分割。准确的骨分割对于手术计划和解剖分析非常重要，但现有的基于 3D 体素的模型（例如 nnU-Net 和 STU-Net）需要大量计算，并且每次扫描通常需要几分钟，这限制了时间紧迫的使用。所提出的 Bonnet 通过集成一系列新颖的框架组件来解决这个问题，包括基于 HU 的骨骼阈值、基于稀疏 spc​​onv 的 U-Net 的分片推理以及多窗口融合到全卷预测中。 Bonnet 在 TotalSegmentator 上进行训练，并在没有对 RibSeg、CT-Pelvic1K 和 CT-Spine1K 进行额外调整的情况下进行评估，在肋骨、骨盆和脊柱上实现了高 Dice，同时在 RTX A6000 上每次扫描仅需 2.69 秒。与强体素基线相比，Bonnet 获得了相似的精度，但在相同的硬件和平铺设置上将推理时间减少了大约 25 倍。该工具包和预训练模型将在 https://github.com/HINTLab/Bonnet 发布。
> **Abstract**: This work proposes Bonnet, an ultra-fast sparse-volume pipeline for whole-body bone segmentation from CT scans. Accurate bone segmentation is important for surgical planning and anatomical analysis, but existing 3D voxel-based models such as nnU-Net and STU-Net require heavy computation and often take several minutes per scan, which limits time-critical use. The proposed Bonnet addresses this by integrating a series of novel framework components including HU-based bone thresholding, patch-wise inference with a sparse spconv-based U-Net, and multi-window fusion into a full-volume prediction. Trained on TotalSegmentator and evaluated without additional tuning on RibSeg, CT-Pelvic1K, and CT-Spine1K, Bonnet achieves high Dice across ribs, pelvis, and spine while running in only 2.69 seconds per scan on an RTX A6000. Compared to strong voxel baselines, Bonnet attains a similar accuracy but reduces inference time by roughly 25x on the same hardware and tiling setup. The toolkit and pre-trained models will be released at https://github.com/HINTLab/Bonnet.

【7】EndoCaver: Handling Fog, Blur and Glare in Endoscopic Images via Joint Deblurring-Segmentation
- **标题**: EndoCaver：通过联合去模糊分割处理内窥镜图像中的雾、模糊和眩光
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22537
> **作者**: Zhuoyu Wu,Wenhui Ou,Pei-Sze Tan,Jiayan Yang,Wenqi Fang,Zheng Wang,Raphaël C. -W. Phan
> **摘要**: 内窥镜图像分析对于结直肠癌筛查至关重要，但现实条件下经常会出现镜头起雾、运动模糊和镜面高光的问题，这严重影响了自动息肉检测。我们提出了 EndoCaver，一种具有单向引导双解码器架构的轻量级转换器，能够实现图像去模糊和分割的联合多任务功能，同时显着降低计算复杂性和模型参数。具体来说，它集成了用于跨尺度聚合的全局注意力模块（GAM）、用于传输恢复线索的去模糊分割对齐器（DSA）以及用于稳定多任务优化的基于余弦的调度器（LoCoS）。在 Kvasir-SEG 数据集上的实验表明，EndoCaver 在干净数据上达到了 0.922 Dice，在严重图像退化下达到了 0.889，超越了最先进的方法，同时将模型参数减少了 90%。这些结果证明了其效率和稳健性，使其非常适合设备上的临床部署。代码可在 https://github.com/ReaganWu/EndoCaver 获取。
> **Abstract**: Endoscopic image analysis is vital for colorectal cancer screening, yet real-world conditions often suffer from lens fogging, motion blur, and specular highlights, which severely compromise automated polyp detection. We propose EndoCaver, a lightweight transformer with a unidirectional-guided dual-decoder architecture, enabling joint multi-task capability for image deblurring and segmentation while significantly reducing computational complexity and model parameters. Specifically, it integrates a Global Attention Module (GAM) for cross-scale aggregation, a Deblurring-Segmentation Aligner (DSA) to transfer restoration cues, and a cosine-based scheduler (LoCoS) for stable multi-task optimisation. Experiments on the Kvasir-SEG dataset show that EndoCaver achieves 0.922 Dice on clean data and 0.889 under severe image degradation, surpassing state-of-the-art methods while reducing model parameters by 90%. These results demonstrate its efficiency and robustness, making it well-suited for on-device clinical deployment. Code is available at https://github.com/ReaganWu/EndoCaver.

【8】A Survey on Semantic Communication for Vision: Categories, Frameworks, Enabling Techniques, and Applications
- **标题**: 视觉语义沟通调查：类别、框架、支持技术和应用
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22202
> **作者**: Runze Cheng,Yao Sun,Ahmad Taha,Xuesong Liu,David Flynn,Muhammad Ali Imran
> **摘要**: 语义通信（SemCom）作为流量密集型视觉数据传输的变革范例而出现，将焦点从原始数据转移到有意义的内容传输，并缓解了通信资源日益增加的压力。然而，要实现 SemCom，在视觉数据的准确语义量化、不同任务和目标下的鲁棒语义提取和重建、收发器与有效知识利用的协调以及对不可预测的无线通信环境的适应等方面面临着挑战。在本文中，我们对用于视觉数据传输的 SemCom (SemCom-Vision) 进行了系统综述，其中进行了计算机视觉 (CV) 和通信工程相结合的跨学科分析，为机器学习 (ML) 赋能的 SemCom-Vision 设计提供全面的指导。具体来说，本次调查首先阐明了 SemCom 的基础知识和关键概念。然后，我们引入一种新颖的分类视角，根据通过语义量化方案解释的通信目标，将现有的 SemCom-Vision 方法分类为语义保留通信（SPC）、语义扩展通信（SEC）和语义细化通信（SRC）。此外，本次调查还阐述了每个 SemCom-Vision 类别的基于 ML 的编码器-解码器模型和训练算法，以及知识结构和利用策略。最后，我们讨论潜在的 SemCom-Vision 应用。
> **Abstract**: Semantic communication (SemCom) emerges as a transformative paradigm for traffic-intensive visual data transmission, shifting focus from raw data to meaningful content transmission and relieving the increasing pressure on communication resources. However, to achieve SemCom, challenges are faced in accurate semantic quantization for visual data, robust semantic extraction and reconstruction under diverse tasks and goals, transceiver coordination with effective knowledge utilization, and adaptation to unpredictable wireless communication environments. In this paper, we present a systematic review of SemCom for visual data transmission (SemCom-Vision), wherein an interdisciplinary analysis integrating computer vision (CV) and communication engineering is conducted to provide comprehensive guidelines for the machine learning (ML)-empowered SemCom-Vision design. Specifically, this survey first elucidates the basics and key concepts of SemCom. Then, we introduce a novel classification perspective to categorize existing SemCom-Vision approaches as semantic preservation communication (SPC), semantic expansion communication (SEC), and semantic refinement communication (SRC) based on communication goals interpreted through semantic quantization schemes. Moreover, this survey articulates the ML-based encoder-decoder models and training algorithms for each SemCom-Vision category, followed by knowledge structure and utilization strategies. Finally, we discuss potential SemCom-Vision applications.

【9】SCENE: Semantic-aware Codec Enhancement with Neural Embeddings
- **标题**: 场景：通过神经嵌入增强语义感知编解码器
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22189
> **作者**: Han-Yu Lin,Li-Wei Chen,Hung-Shin Lee
> **摘要**: 标准视频编解码器的压缩伪影通常会降低感知质量。我们提出了一种轻量级、语义感知的预处理框架，通过有选择地解决这些扭曲来增强感知保真度。我们的方法将视觉语言模型的语义嵌入集成到高效的卷积架构中，优先保留感知上重要的结构。该模型使用可微编解码器代理进行端到端训练，使其能够在不修改现有视频管道的情况下减轻各种标准编解码器的伪影。在推理过程中，编解码器代理被丢弃，SCENE 作为独立的预处理器运行，从而实现实时性能。高分辨率基准的实验表明，客观 (MS-SSIM) 和感知 (VMAF) 指标的性能均优于基线，并且在保留显着区域内的详细纹理方面具有显着收益。我们的结果表明，语义引导、编解码器感知的预处理是增强压缩视频流的有效方法。
> **Abstract**: Compression artifacts from standard video codecs often degrade perceptual quality. We propose a lightweight, semantic-aware pre-processing framework that enhances perceptual fidelity by selectively addressing these distortions. Our method integrates semantic embeddings from a vision-language model into an efficient convolutional architecture, prioritizing the preservation of perceptually significant structures. The model is trained end-to-end with a differentiable codec proxy, enabling it to mitigate artifacts from various standard codecs without modifying the existing video pipeline. During inference, the codec proxy is discarded, and SCENE operates as a standalone pre-processor, enabling real-time performance. Experiments on high-resolution benchmarks show improved performance over baselines in both objective (MS-SSIM) and perceptual (VMAF) metrics, with notable gains in preserving detailed textures within salient regions. Our results show that semantic-guided, codec-aware pre-processing is an effective approach for enhancing compressed video streams.

## 系统与控制(eess.SY:Systems and Control)

【1】Reinforcement Learning-Based Co-Design and Operation of Chiller and Thermal Energy Storage for Cost-Optimal HVAC Systems
- **标题**: 基于强化学习的制冷机和热能存储的协同设计和运行，实现成本优化的 HVAC 系统
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22880
> **作者**: Tanay Raghunandan Srinivasa,Vivek Deulkar,Aviruch Bhatia,Vishal Garg
> **摘要**: 我们使用强化学习研究商业 HVAC 系统冷却基础设施的联合运行和规模调整，目标是在 30 年的时间内最大限度地降低生命周期成本。冷却系统由固定容量的冷水机组和热能存储（TES）机组组成，联合运行以满足时变电价下的随机每小时冷却需求。生命周期成本包括资本支出和贴现运营成本，包括电力消耗和维护。资本成本的严重不对称产生了一个关键挑战：增加一台冷水机容量比同等增加 TES 容量要昂贵得多。因此，确定冷水机组和 TES 尺寸的正确组合，同时确保最佳运行下的零冷却负载损失，是一个重要的协同设计问题。为了解决这个问题，我们将固定基础设施配置的冷水机组运行问题表述为有限视野马尔可夫决策过程（MDP），其中控制行为是冷水机组部分负载比（PLR）。使用具有受限动作空间的深度 Q 网络 (DQN) 来求解 MDP。学习到的 DQN RL 政策可在需求和电价降温的历史记录中最大限度地降低电力成本。对于每个候选冷却器-TES 大小配置，都会评估经过训练的策略。然后，我们将注意力集中在完全满足冷却需求的配置上，并在此可行的集合上执行生命周期成本最小化，以确定成本最优的基础设施设计。使用这种方法，我们确定最佳制冷机和热能存储容量分别为 700 和 1500。
> **Abstract**: We study the joint operation and sizing of cooling infrastructure for commercial HVAC systems using reinforcement learning, with the objective of minimizing life-cycle cost over a 30-year horizon. The cooling system consists of a fixed-capacity electric chiller and a thermal energy storage (TES) unit, jointly operated to meet stochastic hourly cooling demands under time-varying electricity prices. The life-cycle cost accounts for both capital expenditure and discounted operating cost, including electricity consumption and maintenance. A key challenge arises from the strong asymmetry in capital costs: increasing chiller capacity by one unit is far more expensive than an equivalent increase in TES capacity. As a result, identifying the right combination of chiller and TES sizes, while ensuring zero loss-of-cooling-load under optimal operation, is a non-trivial co-design problem. To address this, we formulate the chiller operation problem for a fixed infrastructure configuration as a finite-horizon Markov Decision Process (MDP), in which the control action is the chiller part-load ratio (PLR). The MDP is solved using a Deep Q Network (DQN) with a constrained action space. The learned DQN RL policy minimizes electricity cost over historical traces of cooling demand and electricity prices. For each candidate chiller-TES sizing configuration, the trained policy is evaluated. We then restrict attention to configurations that fully satisfy the cooling demand and perform a life-cycle cost minimization over this feasible set to identify the cost-optimal infrastructure design. Using this approach, we determine the optimal chiller and thermal energy storage capacities to be 700 and 1500, respectively.

【2】Degradation-Aware Frequency Regulation of a Heterogeneous Battery Fleet via Reinforcement Learning
- **标题**: 通过强化学习对异构电池组进行退化感知频率调节
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22865
> **作者**: Tanay Raghunandan Srinivasa,Vivek Deulkar,Jia Bhargava,Mohammad Hajiesmaili,Prashant Shenoy
> **摘要**: 电池储能系统越来越多地被部署为快速响应资源，用于电网平衡服务（例如频率调节）和减轻可再生能源发电的不确定性。然而，重复充电和放电会导致循环退化并缩短电池寿命。本文研究了异构电池组的实时调度，该电池组共同跟踪受每个电池斜坡率和容量限制影响的随机平衡信号，同时最大限度地减少长期循环退化。循环退化基本上是路径相关的：它由充电状态 (SoC) 轨迹形成的充电-放电循环决定，并且通常通过雨流循环计数来量化。这种非马尔可夫结构使得很难将退化表示为附加的每时间步成本，从而使经典的动态规划方法变得复杂。我们通过将车队调度问题制定为具有受限行动空间的马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）并设计密集代理奖励来解决这一挑战，该代理奖励在每个时间步骤提供信息反馈，同时与长期循环深度减少保持一致。为了将学习扩展到由细粒度 SoC 离散化和不对称每电池约束引起的大型状态动作空间，我们开发了一种函数逼近强化学习方法，使用极限学习机 (ELM) 作为随机非线性特征图并结合线性时差学习。我们在玩具马尔可夫信号模型和从特拉华大学获得的真实世界调节信号轨迹训练的马尔可夫模型上评估了所提出的方法，并证明与基线调度策略相比，周期深度发生和退化指标的持续减少。
> **Abstract**: Battery energy storage systems are increasingly deployed as fast-responding resources for grid balancing services such as frequency regulation and for mitigating renewable generation uncertainty. However, repeated charging and discharging induces cycling degradation and reduces battery lifetime. This paper studies the real-time scheduling of a heterogeneous battery fleet that collectively tracks a stochastic balancing signal subject to per-battery ramp-rate and capacity constraints, while minimizing long-term cycling degradation. Cycling degradation is fundamentally path-dependent: it is determined by charge-discharge cycles formed by the state-of-charge (SoC) trajectory and is commonly quantified via rainflow cycle counting. This non-Markovian structure makes it difficult to express degradation as an additive per-time-step cost, complicating classical dynamic programming approaches. We address this challenge by formulating the fleet scheduling problem as a Markov decision process (MDP) with constrained action space and designing a dense proxy reward that provides informative feedback at each time step while remaining aligned with long-term cycle-depth reduction. To scale learning to large state-action spaces induced by fine-grained SoC discretization and asymmetric per-battery constraints, we develop a function-approximation reinforcement learning method using an Extreme Learning Machine (ELM) as a random nonlinear feature map combined with linear temporal-difference learning. We evaluate the proposed approach on a toy Markovian signal model and on a Markovian model trained from real-world regulation signal traces obtained from the University of Delaware, and demonstrate consistent reductions in cycle-depth occurrence and degradation metrics compared to baseline scheduling policies.

## 历史与概述(math.HO:History and Overview)

【1】Proliferating series by Jean Barraqué: a study and classification in mathematical terms
- **标题**: Jean Barraqué 的增殖系列：数学术语的研究和分类
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22176
> **作者**: Isabel Tardón,Pablo Martín-Santamaría
> **摘要**: 巴拉克的增殖系列通过在构建系列时创造了一个新的不变量，对经典序列主义的概念进行了有趣的转变：在构建给定基本系列的扩散过程中，保持不变的不是连续音符之间的间隔，而是两个连续系列之间发生的音符的排列，也就是说，系列中音符顺序的转换。这为对串行方法感兴趣的作曲家提供了新的可能性，因为通过这种方法获得的音程多样性远远大于经典串行方法。在这份手稿中，我们将从数学的角度研究激增的系列所提供的一些未经探索的可能性，这将使作曲家更加熟悉它们，并可能导致创作出将系列主义提升到新水平的作品。
> **Abstract**: Barraqué's proliferating series give an interesting turn on the concept of classic serialism by creating a new invariant when it comes to constructing the series: rather than the intervals between consecutive notes, what remains unaltered during the construction of the proliferations of the given base series is the permutation of the notes which happens between two consecutive series, that is to say, the transformation of the order of the notes in the series. This presents new possibilities for composers interested in the serial method, given the fact that the variety of intervals obtained by this method is far greater than that of classic serialism. In this manuscript, we will study some unexplored possibilities that the proliferating series offer from a mathematical point of view, which will allow composers to gain much more familiarity with them and potentially result in the creation of pieces that take serialism to the next level.

## 数值分析(math.NA:Numerical Analysis)

【1】Bayesian Interpolating Neural Network (B-INN): a scalable and reliable Bayesian model for large-scale physical systems
- **标题**: 贝叶斯插值神经网络 (B-INN)：适用于大规模物理系统的可扩展且可靠的贝叶斯模型
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22860
> **作者**: Chanwook Park,Brian Kim,Jiachen Guo,Wing Kam Liu
> **摘要**: 与确定性模型相比，用于不确定性量化的神经网络和机器学习模型的可扩展性有限且可靠性较差。在行业规模的主动学习环境中，生成单个高保真模拟可能需要数天或数周的计算，并产生千兆字节数量级的数据量，它们很快就变得不切实际。本文提出了一种可扩展且可靠的贝叶斯代理模型，称为贝叶斯插值神经网络（B-INN）。 B-INN将高阶插值理论与张量分解和交替方向算法相结合，能够在不影响预测精度的情况下有效降维。我们从理论上证明，B-INN 的函数空间是高斯过程的子集，而其贝叶斯推理相对于训练样本的数量呈现线性复杂度 $\mathcal{O}(N)$。数值实验表明，与贝叶斯神经网络和高斯过程相比，通过稳健的不确定性估计，B-INN 的速度可以快 20 倍到 10,000 倍。这些功能使 B-INN 成为大规模工业模拟中不确定性驱动的主动学习的实用基础，其中计算效率和稳健的不确定性校准至关重要。
> **Abstract**: Neural networks and machine learning models for uncertainty quantification suffer from limited scalability and poor reliability compared to their deterministic counterparts. In industry-scale active learning settings, where generating a single high-fidelity simulation may require days or weeks of computation and produce data volumes on the order of gigabytes, they quickly become impractical. This paper proposes a scalable and reliable Bayesian surrogate model, termed the Bayesian Interpolating Neural Network (B-INN). The B-INN combines high-order interpolation theory with tensor decomposition and alternating direction algorithm to enable effective dimensionality reduction without compromising predictive accuracy. We theoretically show that the function space of a B-INN is a subset of that of Gaussian processes, while its Bayesian inference exhibits linear complexity, $\mathcal{O}(N)$, with respect to the number of training samples. Numerical experiments demonstrate that B-INNs can be from 20 times to 10,000 times faster with a robust uncertainty estimation compared to Bayesian neural networks and Gaussian processes. These capabilities make B-INN a practical foundation for uncertainty-driven active learning in large-scale industrial simulations, where computational efficiency and robust uncertainty calibration are paramount.

## 大气和海洋物理(physics.ao-ph:Atmospheric and Oceanic Physics)

【1】AI Decodes Historical Chinese Archives to Reveal Lost Climate History
- **标题**: 人工智能解码中国历史档案，揭示失落的气候历史
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22458
> **作者**: Sida He,Lingxi Xie,Xiaopeng Zhang,Qi Tian
> **摘要**: 历史档案包含气候事件的定性描述，但将其转化为定量记录仍然是一项根本挑战。在这里，我们引入了一种范式转变：一种生成式人工智能框架，它通过推断与记录事件相关的定量气候模式来颠倒历史编年史的逻辑。应用于中国历史档案，它可以重建公元 1368 年至 1911 年期间中国东南部的亚年降水量。我们的重建不仅量化了明代大旱等标志性极端事件，更重要的是，绘制了五个世纪以来厄尔尼诺现象对该地区降水影响的完整空间和季节结构，揭示了较短的现代记录中无法获得的动态。我们的方法和高分辨率气候数据集直接适用于气候科学，并对历史和社会科学具有更广泛的影响。
> **Abstract**: Historical archives contain qualitative descriptions of climate events, yet converting these into quantitative records has remained a fundamental challenge. Here we introduce a paradigm shift: a generative AI framework that inverts the logic of historical chroniclers by inferring the quantitative climate patterns associated with documented events. Applied to historical Chinese archives, it produces the sub-annual precipitation reconstruction for southeastern China over the period 1368-1911 AD. Our reconstruction not only quantifies iconic extremes like the Ming Dynasty's Great Drought but also, crucially, maps the full spatial and seasonal structure of El Ni$ñ$o influence on precipitation in this region over five centuries, revealing dynamics inaccessible in shorter modern records. Our methodology and high-resolution climate dataset are directly applicable to climate science and have broader implications for the historical and social sciences.

## 化学物理(physics.chem-ph:Chemical Physics)

【1】A Cross-Domain Graph Learning Protocol for Single-Step Molecular Geometry Refinement
- **标题**: 用于单步分子几何精修的跨域图学习协议
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22723
> **作者**: Chengchun Liu,Wendi Cai,Boxuan Zhao,Fanyang Mo
> **摘要**: 准确的分子几何形状是可靠的量子化学预测的先决条件，但密度泛函理论（DFT）优化仍然是高通量分子筛选的主要瓶颈。在这里，我们提出了 GeoOpt-Net，一个多分支 SE(3) 等变几何细化网络，它从在低成本力场水平生成的廉价初始构象异构体开始，在单次正向传递中预测 B3LYP/TZVP 理论水平的 DFT 质量结构。 GeoOpt-Net 使用两阶段策略进行训练，其中广泛预训练的几何表示随后进行微调以接近 B3LYP/TZVP 级别的精度，并通过保真度感知特征调制 (FAFM) 机制实现理论和基础集感知校准。对跨越经典构象异构体生成 (RDKit)、半经验量子方法 (xTB)、数据驱动的几何细化管道 (Auto3D) 和外部类药物分子的机器学习原子间势 (UMA) 等代表性方法进行基准测试表明，GeoOpt-Net 实现了亚毫埃全原子 RMSD，且 B3LYP/TZVP 单点能量偏差接近于零，这表明 DFT 就绪的几何形状可以紧密再现结构和充满活力的参考。除了几何指标之外，GeoOpt-Net 还生成与 DFT 收敛标准本质上兼容的初始猜测，产生非零的“全是”收敛率（宽松阈值下为 65.0%，默认阈值下为 33.4%），并大大减少了重新优化步骤和挂钟时间。 GeoOpt-Net 进一步展示了分子复杂性的平滑且可预测的能量缩放，同时保留了偶极矩等关键电子可观测值。总的来说，这些结果将 GeoOpt-Net 确立为一个可扩展、物理一致的几何细化框架，能够有效加速基于 DFT 的量子化学工作流程。
> **Abstract**: Accurate molecular geometries are a prerequisite for reliable quantum-chemical predictions, yet density functional theory (DFT) optimization remains a major bottleneck for high-throughput molecular screening. Here we present GeoOpt-Net, a multi-branch SE(3)-equivariant geometry refinement network that predicts DFT-quality structures at the B3LYP/TZVP level of theory in a single forward pass starting from inexpensive initial conformers generated at a low-cost force-field level. GeoOpt-Net is trained using a two-stage strategy in which a broadly pretrained geometric representation is subsequently fine-tuned to approach B3LYP/TZVP-level accuracy, with theory- and basis-set-aware calibration enabled by a fidelity-aware feature modulation (FAFM) mechanism. Benchmarking against representative approaches spanning classical conformer generation (RDKit), semiempirical quantum methods (xTB), data-driven geometry refinement pipelines (Auto3D), and machine-learning interatomic potentials (UMA) on external drug-like molecules demonstrates that GeoOpt-Net achieves sub-milli-Å all-atom RMSD with near-zero B3LYP/TZVP single-point energy deviations, indicating DFT-ready geometries that closely reproduce both structural and energetic references. Beyond geometric metrics, GeoOpt-Net generates initial guesses intrinsically compatible with DFT convergence criteria, yielding nonzero ``All-YES'' convergence rates (65.0\% under loose and 33.4\% under default thresholds), and substantially reducing re-optimization steps and wall-clock time. GeoOpt-Net further exhibits smooth and predictable energy scaling with molecular complexity while preserving key electronic observables such as dipole moments. Collectively, these results establish GeoOpt-Net as a scalable, physically consistent geometry refinement framework that enables efficient acceleration of DFT-based quantum-chemical workflows.

## 基因组学(q-bio.GN:Genomics)

【1】Beyond Conditional Computation: Retrieval-Augmented Genomic Foundation Models with Gengram
- **标题**: 超越条件计算：使用 Gengram 进行检索增强的基因组基础模型
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22203
> **作者**: Huinan Xu,Xuyang Feng,Junhong Chen,Junchen Liu,Kaiwen Deng,Kai Ding,Shengning Long,Jiaxue Shuai,Zhaorong Li,Shiping Liu,Guirong Xue,Zhan Xiao
> **摘要**: 当前的基因组基础模型（GFM）依赖于广泛的神经计算来隐式地近似来自单核苷酸输入的保守生物基序。我们提出了 Gengram，这是一种条件记忆模块，它通过基因组特定的哈希方案引入了针对多碱基基序的显式且高效的查找原语，从而建立了基因组“语法”。 Gengram 集成到最先进的 GFM 的骨干中，在多项功能基因组学任务中取得了显着的成果（高达 14%）。该模块展示了强大的架构泛化，同时对 Gengram 潜在空间的进一步检查揭示了与基础生物学知识密切相关的有意义的表示的出现。通过将结构化主题记忆建立为建模原语，Gengram 同时提高了经验性能和机械可解释性，为下一代 GFM 提供了可扩展且符合生物学的途径。代码可在 https://github.com/zhejianlab/Genos 获取，模型检查点可在 https://huggingface.co/ZhejianLab/Gengram 获取。
> **Abstract**: Current genomic foundation models (GFMs) rely on extensive neural computation to implicitly approximate conserved biological motifs from single-nucleotide inputs. We propose Gengram, a conditional memory module that introduces an explicit and highly efficient lookup primitive for multi-base motifs via a genomic-specific hashing scheme, establishing genomic "syntax". Integrated into the backbone of state-of-the-art GFMs, Gengram achieves substantial gains (up to 14%) across several functional genomics tasks. The module demonstrates robust architectural generalization, while further inspection of Gengram's latent space reveals the emergence of meaningful representations that align closely with fundamental biological knowledge. By establishing structured motif memory as a modeling primitive, Gengram simultaneously boosts empirical performance and mechanistic interpretability, providing a scalable and biology-aligned pathway for the next generation of GFMs. The code is available at https://github.com/zhejianglab/Genos, and the model checkpoint is available at https://huggingface.co/ZhejiangLab/Gengram.

## 计算金融(q-fin.CP:Computational Finance)

【1】Alpha Discovery via Grammar-Guided Learning and Search
- **标题**: 通过语法引导学习和搜索进行 Alpha 发现
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22119
> **作者**: Han Yang,Dong Hao,Zhuohan Wang,Qi Shi,Xingtong Li
> **摘要**: 自动发现公式化的阿尔法因子是量化金融的核心问题。现有方法通常忽略句法和语义约束，依赖于对非结构化和无界空间的穷举搜索。我们提出了 AlphaCFG，一个基于语法的框架，用于定义和发现语法上有效、财务上可解释且计算高效的 alpha 因子。 AlphaCFG 使用面向 alpha 的上下文无关语法来定义树结构、大小控制的搜索空间，并将 alpha 发现制定为树结构的语言马尔可夫决策过程，然后使用由语法敏感的值和策略网络引导的语法感知蒙特卡罗树搜索来解决。对中国和美国股票市场数据集的实验表明，AlphaCFG 在搜索效率和交易盈利能力方面均优于最先进的基线。除了交易策略之外，AlphaCFG 还充当量化金融领域符号因子发现和细化的通用框架，包括资产定价和投资组合构建。
> **Abstract**: Automatically discovering formulaic alpha factors is a central problem in quantitative finance. Existing methods often ignore syntactic and semantic constraints, relying on exhaustive search over unstructured and unbounded spaces. We present AlphaCFG, a grammar-based framework for defining and discovering alpha factors that are syntactically valid, financially interpretable, and computationally efficient. AlphaCFG uses an alpha-oriented context-free grammar to define a tree-structured, size-controlled search space, and formulates alpha discovery as a tree-structured linguistic Markov decision process, which is then solved using a grammar-aware Monte Carlo Tree Search guided by syntax-sensitive value and policy networks. Experiments on Chinese and U.S. stock market datasets show that AlphaCFG outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in both search efficiency and trading profitability. Beyond trading strategies, AlphaCFG serves as a general framework for symbolic factor discovery and refinement across quantitative finance, including asset pricing and portfolio construction.

## 一般财务(q-fin.GN:General Finance)

【1】UniFinEval: Towards Unified Evaluation of Financial Multimodal Models across Text, Images and Videos
- **标题**: UniFinEval：跨文本、图像和视频的金融多模态模型的统一评估
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22162
> **作者**: Zhi Yang,Lingfeng Zeng,Fangqi Lou,Qi Qi,Wei Zhang,Zhenyu Wu,Zhenxiong Yu,Jun Han,Zhiheng Jin,Lejie Zhang,Xiaoming Huang,Xiaolong Liang,Zheng Wei,Junbo Zou,Dongpo Cheng,Zhaowei Liu,Xin Guo,Rongjunchen Zhang,Liwen Zhang
> **摘要**: 多模态大语言模型在赋能金融领域发挥着越来越重要的作用，但其面临的多模态、高密度信息、跨模态多跳推理等挑战超出了现有多模态基准的评估范围。为了解决这一差距，我们提出了 UniFinEval，这是第一个专为高信息密度金融环境而设计的统一多模式基准，涵盖文本、图像和视频。 UniFinEval系统地构建了基于现实金融系统的五个核心财务场景：财务报表审计、公司基本面推理、行业趋势洞察、金融风险感知和资产配置分析。我们手动构建了一个由 3,767 个中英文问答对组成的高质量数据集，并在零样本和 CoT 设置下系统地评估了 10 个主流 MLLM。结果显示，Gemini-3-pro-preview 取得了最佳的整体性能，但与金融专家相比仍存在较大差距。进一步的误差分析揭示了当前模型的系统缺陷。 UniFinEval 旨在对 MLLM 在细粒度、高信息密度的金融环境中的能力进行系统评估，从而增强 MLLM 在现实金融场景中应用的稳健性。数据和代码可在 https://github.com/aifinlab/UniFinEval 获取。
> **Abstract**: Multimodal large language models are playing an increasingly significant role in empowering the financial domain, however, the challenges they face, such as multimodal and high-density information and cross-modal multi-hop reasoning, go beyond the evaluation scope of existing multimodal benchmarks. To address this gap, we propose UniFinEval, the first unified multimodal benchmark designed for high-information-density financial environments, covering text, images, and videos. UniFinEval systematically constructs five core financial scenarios grounded in real-world financial systems: Financial Statement Auditing, Company Fundamental Reasoning, Industry Trend Insights, Financial Risk Sensing, and Asset Allocation Analysis. We manually construct a high-quality dataset consisting of 3,767 question-answer pairs in both chinese and english and systematically evaluate 10 mainstream MLLMs under Zero-Shot and CoT settings. Results show that Gemini-3-pro-preview achieves the best overall performance, yet still exhibits a substantial gap compared to financial experts. Further error analysis reveals systematic deficiencies in current models. UniFinEval aims to provide a systematic assessment of MLLMs' capabilities in fine-grained, high-information-density financial environments, thereby enhancing the robustness of MLLMs applications in real-world financial scenarios. Data and code are available at https://github.com/aifinlab/UniFinEval.

## 风险管理(q-fin.RM:Risk Management)

【1】Stablecoin Design with Adversarial-Robust Multi-Agent Systems via Trust-Weighted Signal Aggregation
- **标题**: 通过信任加权信号聚合进行具有对抗性鲁棒多代理系统的稳定币设计
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22168
> **作者**: Shengwei You,Aditya Joshi,Andrey Kuehlkamp,Jarek Nabrzyski
> **摘要**: 算法稳定币通过程序性储备管理维持目标挂钩，从而保证去中心化的货币稳定性。然而，他们的储备控制器仍然容易受到制度盲目优化的影响，根据晴天数据校准风险参数，同时忽略导致级联故障的尾部事件。 2020 年 3 月的黑色星期四崩盘，其中 MakerDAO 的抵押品拍卖产生了 830 万美元的损失和 15% 的挂钩偏差，暴露了一个关键差距：SAS 等现有模型系统地从协方差估计中忽略了极端波动机制，产生了预期最优的分配，但在对抗压力下却是灾难性的。我们提出了 MVF-Composer，这是一种信任加权均值方差前沿储备控制器，结合了用于风险状态估计的新型应力线束。我们的主要见解是将多代理模拟部署为对抗性压力测试器：异构代理（交易者、流动性提供者、攻击者）在危机场景下执行协议操作，在储备漏洞在链上显现之前暴露出来。我们形式化了一种信任评分机制 T: A -> [0,1]，该机制降低了来自表现出操纵行为的代理的信号的权重，确保风险状态估计器对信号注入和 Sybil 攻击保持稳健。在 1,200 个注入黑天鹅冲击的随机场景中（10% 抵押品回撤、50% 情绪崩溃、协调赎回攻击），相对于 SAS 基线，MVF-Composer 将峰值挂钩偏差降低了 57%，平均恢复时间缩短了 3.1 倍。消融研究证实，信任层在对抗条件下贡献了 23% 的稳定性增益，实现了 72% 的对抗代理检测。我们的系统在商品硬件上运行，除了标准价格供给之外不需要任何链上预言机，并为 DeFi 储备政策的压力测试提供可重复的框架。
> **Abstract**: Algorithmic stablecoins promise decentralized monetary stability by maintaining a target peg through programmatic reserve management. Yet, their reserve controllers remain vulnerable to regime-blind optimization, calibrating risk parameters on fair-weather data while ignoring tail events that precipitate cascading failures. The March 2020 Black Thursday collapse, wherein MakerDAO's collateral auctions yielded $8.3M in losses and a 15% peg deviation, exposed a critical gap: existing models like SAS systematically omit extreme volatility regimes from covariance estimates, producing allocations optimal in expectation but catastrophic under adversarial stress. We present MVF-Composer, a trust-weighted Mean-Variance Frontier reserve controller incorporating a novel Stress Harness for risk-state estimation. Our key insight is deploying multi-agent simulations as adversarial stress-testers: heterogeneous agents (traders, liquidity providers, attackers) execute protocol actions under crisis scenarios, exposing reserve vulnerabilities before they manifest on-chain. We formalize a trust-scoring mechanism T: A -> [0,1] that down-weights signals from agents exhibiting manipulative behavior, ensuring the risk-state estimator remains robust to signal injection and Sybil attacks. Across 1,200 randomized scenarios with injected Black-Swan shocks (10% collateral drawdown, 50% sentiment collapse, coordinated redemption attacks), MVF-Composer reduces peak peg deviation by 57% and mean recovery time by 3.1x relative to SAS baselines. Ablation studies confirm the trust layer accounts for 23% of stability gains under adversarial conditions, achieving 72% adversarial agent detection. Our system runs on commodity hardware, requires no on-chain oracles beyond standard price feeds, and provides a reproducible framework for stress-testing DeFi reserve policies.

## 量子物理学(quant-ph:Quantum Physics)

【1】Spectral Filtering for Learning Quantum Dynamics
- **标题**: 用于学习量子动力学的光谱过滤
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22400
> **作者**: Elad Hazan,Annie Marsden
> **摘要**: 学习高维量子系统是一项基本挑战，众所周知，它受到维数诅咒的影响。我们将预测线性响应机制中的量子演化的任务制定为学习具有扇区边界特征值的复值线性动力系统（CLDS）的特定实例——这种设置也包含现代结构化状态空间模型（SSM）。虽然传统的系统识别试图重建完整的系统矩阵（在希尔伯特维中产生指数成本），但我们提出了量子谱滤波，一种将目标转移到不正确的动态学习的方法。利用 Slepian 基的最佳浓度特性，我们证明此类系统的可学习性严格受有效量子维度 $k^*$ 控制，而有效量子维度 $k^*$ 由光谱带宽和存储范围决定。该结果表明，只要频谱有界，复值 LDS 就可以通过独立于环境状态维度的样本和计算复杂度来学习。
> **Abstract**: Learning high-dimensional quantum systems is a fundamental challenge that notoriously suffers from the curse of dimensionality. We formulate the task of predicting quantum evolution in the linear response regime as a specific instance of learning a Complex-Valued Linear Dynamical System (CLDS) with sector-bounded eigenvalues -- a setting that also encompasses modern Structured State Space Models (SSMs). While traditional system identification attempts to reconstruct full system matrices (incurring exponential cost in the Hilbert dimension), we propose Quantum Spectral Filtering, a method that shifts the goal to improper dynamic learning. Leveraging the optimal concentration properties of the Slepian basis, we prove that the learnability of such systems is governed strictly by an effective quantum dimension $k^*$, determined by the spectral bandwidth and memory horizon. This result establishes that complex-valued LDSs can be learned with sample and computational complexity independent of the ambient state dimension, provided their spectrum is bounded.

【2】Practical Evaluation of Quantum Kernel Methods for Radar Micro-Doppler Classification on Noisy Intermediate-Scale Quantum (NISQ) Hardware
- **标题**: 噪声中尺度量子 (NISQ) 硬件上雷达微多普勒分类的量子核方法的实际评估
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22194
> **作者**: Vikas Agnihotri,Jasleen Kaur,Sarvagya Kaushik
> **摘要**: 本文研究了量子支持向量机 (QSVM) 在使用微多普勒特征的雷达空中目标分类中的应用。通过主成分分析 (PCA) 提取和减少经典特征，以实现高效的量子编码。使用完全纠缠的 ZZFeatureMap 将简化的特征向量嵌入到量子内核诱导的特征空间中，并使用基于内核的 QSVM 进行分类。首先在量子模拟器上评估性能，然后在 NISQ 时代的超导量子硬件上进行验证，特别是 IBM Torino（133 量子位）和 IBM Fez（156 量子位）处理器。实验结果表明，QSVM 相对于经典 SVM 基线实现了有竞争力的分类性能，同时在大幅降低的特征维度上运行。硬件实验揭示了噪声、退相干以及测量发射次数对量子核估计的影响，并进一步表明较新的 Heron r2 架构提高了稳定性和保真度。这项研究对基于模拟器和基于硬件的 QSVM 实现进行了系统比较，并强调了在实际雷达信号分类任务中部署量子核方法的可行性和当前局限性。
> **Abstract**: This paper examines the application of a Quantum Support Vector Machine (QSVM) for radarbased aerial target classification using micro-Doppler signatures. Classical features are extracted and reduced via Principal Component Analysis (PCA) to enable efficient quantum encoding. The reduced feature vectors are embedded into a quantum kernel-induced feature space using a fully entangled ZZFeatureMap and classified using a kernel based QSVM. Performance is first evaluated on a quantum simulator and subsequently validated on NISQ-era superconducting quantum hardware, specifically the IBM Torino (133-qubit) and IBM Fez (156-qubit) processors. Experimental results demonstrate that the QSVM achieves competitive classification performance relative to classical SVM baselines while operating on substantially reduced feature dimensionality. Hardware experiments reveal the impact of noise and decoherence and measurement shot count on quantum kernel estimation, and further show improved stability and fidelity on newer Heron r2 architecture. This study provides a systematic comparison between simulator-based and hardware-based QSVM implementations and highlights both the feasibility and current limitations of deploying quantum kernel methods for practical radar signal classification tasks.
